			KnifeBarragePart1.Parent = KnifeBarrageAimModel

			KnifeBarragePart7.Anchored = true
			KnifeBarragePart7.CanCollide = false
			KnifeBarragePart7.Transparency = 1
			KnifeBarragePart7.Parent = KnifeBarrageAimModel
			KnifeBarragePart7.Name = "KnifeBarragePart7"
			wait(0.1)
			if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarrageAimModel") then
				if game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarragePartMain") then
					if game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarragePart1") then
						game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePart1.CFrame = game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
					if game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarragePart2") then
						game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePart2.CFrame = game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(0.9375,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
					if game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarragePart3") then
						game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePart3.CFrame = game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(-0.9375,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
					if game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarragePart4") then
						game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePart4.CFrame = game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(1.875,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
					if game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarragePart5") then
						game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePart5.CFrame = game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(-1.875,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
					if game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarragePart6") then
						game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePart6.CFrame = game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(2.8125,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
					if game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarragePart7") then
						game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePart7.CFrame = game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel.KnifeBarragePartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(-2.8125,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
				end
			end
			wait(0.1)
			XSlashAimModel = Instance.new("Model")
			XSlashAimModel.Parent = game.Workspace
			XSlashAimModel.Name = "XSlashAimModel"
			wait()
			XSlashPartMain = Instance.new("Part")
			XSlashPartMain.Anchored = true
			XSlashPartMain.CanCollide = false
			XSlashPartMain.Transparency = 1
			XSlashPartMain.Parent = XSlashAimModel
			XSlashPartMain.Name = "XSlashPartMain"

			XSlashPart1 = Instance.new("Part")
			XSlashPart1.Anchored = true
			XSlashPart1.CanCollide = false
			XSlashPart1.Transparency = 1
			XSlashPart1.Parent = XSlashAimModel
			XSlashPart1.Name = "XSlashPart1"
			wait()
			XSlashPart2 = Instance.new("Part")
			XSlashPart2.Anchored = true
			XSlashPart2.CanCollide = false
			XSlashPart2.Transparency = 1
			XSlashPart2.Parent = XSlashAimModel
			XSlashPart2.Name = "XSlashPart2"
			wait()
			XSlashPart3 = Instance.new("Part")
			XSlashPart3.Anchored = true
			XSlashPart3.CanCollide = false
			XSlashPart3.Transparency = 1
			XSlashPart3.Parent = XSlashAimModel
			XSlashPart3.Name = "XSlashPart3"
			wait(0.1)
			if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("XSlashAimModel") then
				if game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel:FindFirstChild("XSlashPartMain") then
					if game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel:FindFirstChild("XSlashPart1") then
						game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel.XSlashPart1.CFrame = game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel.XSlashPartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
					if game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel:FindFirstChild("XSlashPart2") then
						game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel.XSlashPart2.CFrame = game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel.XSlashPartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(1.875,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
					if game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel:FindFirstChild("XSlashPart3") then
						game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel.XSlashPart3.CFrame = game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel.XSlashPartMain.CFrame * CFrame.new(-1.875,0,-15) * CFrame.Angles(0.35,math.rad(180),0)
					end
				end
			end
			wait(0.1)
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid").Died:Connect(function()
				KnifeBarrageAimModel:Destroy()
				XSlashAimModel:Destroy()
				MorphingCheck = 0
				currentcharacter = "Human"
			end)
			wait(0.1)
			mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
			cd = 1
			tool = Instance.new("Tool")
			tool.RequiresHandle = false
			tool.Name = 'Knife Barrage'
			tool.ToolTip = "Spawns a knife barrage."
			tool.CanBeDropped = false
			tool.Activated:connect(function()
				local pos = mouse.Hit
				if cd == 1 then
					cd = 0
					if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarrageAimModel") then
						if game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:FindFirstChild("KnifeBarragePartMain") then
							game.Workspace.KnifeBarrageAimModel:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position, pos.Position))
						end
					end
					wait()
					for i, v in pairs(ToolStorage:GetChildren()) do
						if v.Name == "KnifeBarrage1" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(KnifeBarragePart1.Position.X, KnifeBarragePart1.Position.Y, KnifeBarragePart1.Position.Z);
						end
						if v.Name == "KnifeBarrage2" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(KnifeBarragePart2.Position.X, KnifeBarragePart2.Position.Y, KnifeBarragePart2.Position.Z);
						end
						if v.Name == "KnifeBarrage3" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(KnifeBarragePart3.Position.X, KnifeBarragePart3.Position.Y, KnifeBarragePart3.Position.Z);
						end
						if v.Name == "KnifeBarrage4" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(KnifeBarragePart4.Position.X, KnifeBarragePart4.Position.Y, KnifeBarragePart4.Position.Z);
						end
						if v.Name == "KnifeBarrage5" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(KnifeBarragePart5.Position.X, KnifeBarragePart5.Position.Y, KnifeBarragePart5.Position.Z);
						end
						if v.Name == "KnifeBarrage6" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(KnifeBarragePart6.Position.X, KnifeBarragePart6.Position.Y, KnifeBarragePart6.Position.Z);
						end
						if v.Name == "KnifeBarrage7" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(KnifeBarragePart7.Position.X, KnifeBarragePart7.Position.Y, KnifeBarragePart7.Position.Z);
						end
					end
					wait(1.5)
					cd = 1
				end
			end)
			tool.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
			wait()
			mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
			gb2 = 1
			cd2 = 1
			tool2 = Instance.new("Tool")
			tool2.RequiresHandle = false
			tool2.Name = 'Powerful Blaster'
			tool2.ToolTip = "Spawns a Gaster Blaster."
			tool2.CanBeDropped = false
			tool2.Activated:connect(function()
				local pos = mouse.Hit
				if cd2 == 1 then
					if gb2 == 1 then
						cd2 = 0
						for i, v in pairs(ToolStorage:GetChildren()) do
							if v.Name == "PowerfulBlaster1" or v.Name == "PowerfulBlaster2" or v.Name == "PowerfulBlaster3" then
								v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(pos.X,pos.Y,pos.Z);
							end
						end
						wait(1.65)
						gb2 = 2
						cd2 = 1
					elseif gb2 == 2 then
						cd2 = 0
						for i, v in pairs(ToolStorage:GetChildren()) do
							if v.Name == "PowerfulBlaster4" or v.Name == "PowerfulBlaster5" or v.Name == "PowerfulBlaster6" then
								v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(pos.X,pos.Y,pos.Z);
							end
						end
						wait(1.65)
						gb2 = 3
						cd2 = 1
					elseif gb2 == 3 then
						cd2 = 0
						for i, v in pairs(ToolStorage:GetChildren()) do
							if v.Name == "PowerfulBlaster7" or v.Name == "PowerfulBlaster8" or v.Name == "PowerfulBlaster9" then
								v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(pos.X,pos.Y,pos.Z);
							end
						end
						wait(1.65)
						gb2 = 1
						cd2 = 1
					end
				end
			end)
			tool2.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
			wait()
			cd3 = 1
			ToolStorage["X's Blade"].RemoteEvent.Local.Enabled = false
			wait()
			ToolStorage["X's Blade"].Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
			wait()
			Blade = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack["X's Blade"]
			Blade.Activated:connect(function()
				local pos = mouse.Hit
				if cd3 == 1 then
					cd3 = 0
					if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("XSlashAimModel") then
						if game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel:FindFirstChild("XSlashPartMain") then
							game.Workspace.XSlashAimModel:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position, pos.Position))
						end
					end
					wait()
					for i, v in pairs(ToolStorage:GetChildren()) do
						if v.Name == "MidSlash1" or v.Name == "MidSlash2" or v.Name == "MidSlash3" or v.Name == "MidSlash4" or v.Name == "MidSlash5" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(XSlashPart1.Position.X, XSlashPart1.Position.Y, XSlashPart1.Position.Z);
						end
						if v.Name == "LeftSlash1" or v.Name == "LeftSlash2" or v.Name == "LeftSlash3" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(XSlashPart2.Position.X, XSlashPart2.Position.Y, XSlashPart2.Position.Z);
						end
						if v.Name == "RightSlash1" or v.Name == "RightSlash2" or v.Name == "RightSlash3" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(XSlashPart3.Position.X, XSlashPart3.Position.Y, XSlashPart3.Position.Z);
						end
					end
					wait(0.5)
					cd3 = 1
				end
			end)
			wait()
			mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
			cd4 = 1
			tool4 = Instance.new("Tool")
			tool4.RequiresHandle = false
			tool4.Name = 'OVERWRITE'
			tool4.ToolTip = "Spawns an OVERWRITE Zone"
			tool4.CanBeDropped = false
			tool4.Activated:connect(function()
				local pos = Vector3.new(mouse.Hit.X, mouse.Hit.Y - 5.6996, mouse.Hit.Z)
				if cd4 == 1 then
					cd4 = 0
					for i, v in pairs(ToolStorage:GetChildren()) do
						if v.Name == "Overwrite1" or v.Name == "Overwrite2" or v.Name == "Overwrite3" or v.Name == "Overwrite4" or v.Name == "Overwrite5" or v.Name == "Overwrite6" or v.Name == "Overwrite7" or v.Name == "Overwrite8" then
							v.RemoteEvent:FireServer(pos.X, pos.Y, pos.Z);
						end
					end
					wait(90)
					cd4 = 1
				end
			end)
			tool4.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
			wait(0.1)
			if isfile('Spycrabzedz1/PowerfulCross.mp3') then
				wait()
			else
				writefile("Spycrabzedz1/PowerfulCross.mp3",game:HttpGet("https://github.com/GreenySteveyYtt/SpycrabAndzedz1GUI/raw/main/PowerfulCross.mp3"))
			end
			repeat wait() until isfile('Spycrabzedz1/PowerfulCross.mp3')
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Sound.SoundId = getcustomasset("Spycrabzedz1/PowerfulCross.mp3")
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Sound.TimePosition = "0"
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Sound.Volume = "1.5"
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Sound.PlaybackSpeed = "1" --0.75
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid").Died:Connect(function()
				ToolStorage:Destroy()
				KnifeBarrageAimModel:Destroy()
				XSlashAimModel:Destroy()
				currentcharacter = "Human"
				MorphingCheck = 0
			end)
			wait()
			DebouncePowerfulCross = 1
		end
	end
end)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid").Died:Connect(function()
	currentcharacter = "Human"
	MorphingCheck = 0
end)
coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait() do
		if MorphingCheck == 1 then
			if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-7941, 15.5, 108718)
			end
		end
	end
end)()


coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait() do
		if V404Infection.Enabled == true and InfectedSickness.Enabled == true and E404Blind.Enabled == false then
			V404Infection.Parent = game.Workspace
			InfectedSickness.Parent = game.Workspace
			game.Lighting.FinalV404Blindness.Enabled = true
		end
		if V404Infection.Enabled == false and InfectedSickness.Enabled == false then
			V404Infection.Parent = game.Lighting
			InfectedSickness.Parent = game.Lighting
			game.Lighting.FinalV404Blindness.Enabled = false
		end
	end
end)()

coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait(0.1) do
		for _, child in ipairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetDescendants()) do
			if child.Name == "Handle" then
				child.CanTouch = false
				child.CanCollide = false
			end
		end
	end
end)()

coroutine.wrap(function()
	while wait() do
		if CorruptionDefenseEnabled == true then
			if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("CorruptionDefenseHighlight") == nil then
				local DefenseHighlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
				DefenseHighlight.Name = "CorruptionDefenseHighlight"
				DefenseHighlight.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				DefenseHighlight.FillTransparency = 1
				DefenseHighlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(170, 0, 255)
			end
		else
			if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("CorruptionDefenseHighlight") then
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.CorruptionDefenseHighlight:Destroy()
			end
		end
	end
end)()
